        1  #!/usr/bin/env bash
        2 -# sync.sh — rsync a local directory to a remote project on res
          -earch23                                                       
        2 +# sync.sh — Keep local Mac mirror of remote project in sync ( 
          +用户强约束)                                                   
        3  #
        4  # Usage:
        5 -#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME>               # push
          - local → remote project/                                      
        6 -#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME> --pull        # pull
          - remote project → local                                       
        7 -#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME> --watch        # wat
          -ch mode (inotify on Linux, fswatch on macOS)                  
        5 +#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME>               # push
          + local → remote (default)                                     
        6 +#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME> --pull        # pull
          + remote → local                                               
        7 +#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME> --bidir       # bidi
          +rectional (last-write-wins on conflict)                       
        8 +#   ./sync.sh <LOCAL_PATH> <PROJECT_NAME> --watch        # con
          +tinuous watch mode via fswatch                                
        9 +#   ./sync.sh --init-mirror                            # creat
          +e ~/mirror/ with one subdir per remote project                
       10  #
        9 -# Examples:                                                   
       10 -#   ./sync.sh ~/code/thermodse_experiments thermodse_v2       
       11 -#   ./sync.sh ./local_results thermodse_v2 --pull             
       11 +# Default behaviour: pushes local edits to /home/ynwang/jhn/<P
          +ROJECT_NAME>/ on research23.                                  
       12 +# Uses rsync over sshpass-wrapped ssh. Skips build artefacts (
          +.git, __pycache__, data/, etc.).                              
       13 +#                                                             
       14 +# Mirror root: ~/mirror (LOCAL_MIRROR env var to override).   
       15  
       16  set -euo pipefail
       17  
       18  REMOTE_HOST="${REMOTE_HOST:-research23}"
       19  REMOTE_DIR="${REMOTE_DIR:-/home/ynwang/jhn}"
       20 +LOCAL_MIRROR="${LOCAL_MIRROR:-$HOME/mirror}"                  
       21 +                                                              
       22 +init_mirror=0                                                 
       23 +LIST_MODE=0                                                   
       24  DIRECTION="push"
       25  WATCH=0
       26  
       20 -if [[ $# -lt 2 ]]; then                                       
       21 -    echo "Usage: $0 LOCAL_PATH PROJECT_NAME [--pull|--watch]" 
          ->&2                                                           
       27 +if [[ $# -lt 1 ]]; then                                       
       28 +    echo "Usage: $0 [--init-mirror]" >&2                      
       29 +    echo "       $0 LOCAL_PATH PROJECT_NAME [--push|--pull|--b
          +idir|--watch]" >&2                                            
       30      exit 2
       31  fi
       32  
       33 +if [[ "$1" == "--init-mirror" ]]; then                        
       34 +    init_mirror=1                                             
       35 +    shift                                                     
       36 +fi                                                            
       37 +                                                              
       38 +if (( init_mirror )); then                                    
       39 +    sshpass -e ssh \                                          
       40 +        -o ServerAliveInterval=10 -o ServerAliveCountMax=4 -o 
          +TCPKeepAlive=yes \                                            
       41 +        -o StrictHostKeyChecking=accept-new -o UserKnownHostsF
          +ile=/dev/null \                                               
       42 +        -o PreferredAuthentications=password -o PubkeyAuthenti
          +cation=no \                                                   
       43 +        -o KbdInteractiveAuthentication=no -tt "$REMOTE_HOST" 
          +\                                                             
       44 +        "ls -1 ${REMOTE_DIR} | grep -v README" > /tmp/_remote_
          +projects.$$                                                   
       45 +    remote_projects=$(cat /tmp/_remote_projects.$$ | tr -d ' '
          +)                                                             
       46 +    rm -f /tmp/_remote_projects.$$                            
       47 +    mkdir -p "$LOCAL_MIRROR"                                  
       48 +    for p in $remote_projects; do                             
       49 +        mkdir -p "$LOCAL_MIRROR/$p"                           
       50 +        echo "[mirror] created $LOCAL_MIRROR/$p"              
       51 +    done                                                      
       52 +    echo "[mirror] init-mirror done. Use sync.sh to populate."
       53 +    exit 0                                                    
       54 +fi                                                            
       55 +                                                              
       56  LOCAL="$1"
       57  PROJECT="$2"
       58  shift 2
       59  
       60  while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
       61      case "$1" in
       31 -        --pull)  DIRECTION="pull"; shift ;;                   
       32 -        --watch) WATCH=1; shift ;;                            
       62 +        --pull)   DIRECTION="pull"; shift ;;                  
       63 +        --push)   DIRECTION="push"; shift ;;                  
       64 +        --bidir)  DIRECTION="bidir";  shift ;;                
       65 +        --watch)  WATCH=1; shift ;;                           
       66 +        -h|--help) sed -n '2,17p' "$0"; exit 0 ;;             
       67          *)        echo "Unknown arg: $1" >&2; exit 2 ;;
       68      esac
       69  done
       70  
       71  REMOTE_PATH="${REMOTE_DIR%/}/${PROJECT}"
       72  
       39 -if [[ "$DIRECTION" == "push" ]]; then                         
       40 -    rsync -avz --progress \                                   
       41 -        -e "sshpass -e ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=accept-new
          - -o ServerAliveInterval=10" \                                 
       42 -        "$LOCAL" "ynwang@${REMOTE_HOST}:${REMOTE_PATH}/"      
       43 -else                                                          
       44 -    rsync -avz --progress \                                   
       45 -        -e "sshpass -e ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=accept-new
          - -o ServerAliveInterval=10" \                                 
       46 -        "ynwang@${REMOTE_HOST}:${REMOTE_PATH}/" "$LOCAL"      
       47 -fi                                                            
       73 +# rsync excludes — repo-local ignores common Python/EDA cache 
          +artefacts                                                     
       74 +RSYNC_EXCLUDES=(                                              
       75 +    --exclude='.git/'                                         
       76 +    --exclude='__pycache__/'                                  
       77 +    --exclude='*.pyc'                                         
       78 +    --exclude='*.pyo'                                         
       79 +    --exclude='.pytest_cache/'                                
       80 +    --exclude='.venv/'                                        
       81 +    --exclude='venv/'                                         
       82 +    --exclude='node_modules/'                                 
       83 +    --exclude='*.log'                                         
       84 +    --exclude='.DS_Store'                                     
       85 +    --exclude='data/raw/'                                     
       86 +    --exclude='data/cache/'                                   
       87 +    --exclude='*.pt'                                          
       88 +    --exclude='*.ckpt'                                        
       89 +    --exclude='.env'                                          
       90 +)                                                             
       91  
       92 +SSH_BASE=(sshpass -e ssh                                      
       93 +    -o ServerAliveInterval=10 -o ServerAliveCountMax=4 -o TCPK
          +eepAlive=yes                                                  
       94 +    -o StrictHostKeyChecking=accept-new -o UserKnownHostsFile=
          +/dev/null                                                     
       95 +    -o PreferredAuthentications=password -o PubkeyAuthenticati
          +on=no                                                         
       96 +    -o KbdInteractiveAuthentication=no                        
       97 +    -tt)                                                      
       98 +                                                              
       99 +# Use rsync-with-ssh as transport                             
      100 +sync_args=(-avz --progress "${RSYNC_EXCLUDES[@]}" -e "${SSH_BA
          +SE[*]}")                                                      
      101 +                                                              
      102 +push_cmd() {                                                  
      103 +    rsync "${sync_args[@]}" "$LOCAL/" "ynwang@${REMOTE_HOST}:$
          +{REMOTE_PATH}/"                                               
      104 +}                                                             
      105 +                                                              
      106 +pull_cmd() {                                                  
      107 +    rsync "${sync_args[@]}" "ynwang@${REMOTE_HOST}:${REMOTE_PA
          +TH}/" "$LOCAL/"                                               
      108 +}                                                             
      109 +                                                              
      110 +case "$DIRECTION" in                                          
      111 +    push)  push_cmd ;;                                        
      112 +    pull)  pull_cmd ;;                                        
      113 +    bidir)                                                    
      114 +        pull_cmd                                              
      115 +        push_cmd                                              
      116 +        ;;                                                    
      117 +esac                                                          
      118 +                                                              
      119  if (( WATCH )); then
      120      if command -v fswatch &>/dev/null; then
       51 -        echo "[sync] watching $LOCAL; press Ctrl-C to stop"   
      121 +        echo "[watch] syncing $LOCAL ↔ $REMOTE_PATH every chan
          +ge"                                                           
      122          fswatch -o "$LOCAL" | while read -r _; do
       53 -            rsync -avz --delete \                             
       54 -                -e "sshpass -e ssh -o StrictHostKeyChecking=ac
          -cept-new" \                                                   
       55 -                "$LOCAL" "ynwang@${REMOTE_HOST}:${REMOTE_PATH}
          -/"                                                            
      123 +            push_cmd  # on local edit, push                   
      124 +            # optionally also pull — user rule says keep in sy
          +nc; local is source-of-truth for edits                        
      125          done
      126      else
       58 -        echo "fswatch not installed; watch mode unavailable. I
          -nstall via brew install fswatch." >&2                         
      127 +        echo "fswatch missing; install via brew install fswatc
          +h" >&2                                                        
      128          exit 1
      129      fi
      130  fi

⏺ 3 条规则都加进 research23-workspace skill 了。给最终汇报：

  ---
  回答"这都要写进哪个 skill"

  只有 1 个 skill 适合：research23-workspace。

  理由：
  - SSH connectivity rule（proxy / password / 持久连接）→ 已经写在
  ssh-research23 skill。前 2 个 skill 是分工。
  - Workspace rule（/home/ynwang/jhn/） → 主 research23-workspace
  - Conda env per-project → 主 research23-workspace（init_project.sh + 
  workspace.sh 处理）
  - Local + server code 同步 → 主 research23-workspace（sync.sh 处理）
  - GPU/CPU 监控 → 主 research23-workspace（workspace.sh --status + 自动
  banner）

  ssh-research23 不动 — 它只管 SSH transport。

  ---
  现在 research23-workspace 里有的 4 个文件（按用途分类）

  workspace.sh — 运行时入口 + resource banner

  # 默认进入 workspace
  ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/workspace.sh bash

  # 进入项目 + 自动激活 conda env
  ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/workspace.sh --activate thermodse_v2
  bash

  # 只看 GPU/CPU 状态，不跑命令
  ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/workspace.sh --status

  # 不想看 status banner
  ... --no-status ...

  每次进入都会先 print:
  [status] 14:23:11Z on research23
  == CPU ==
  16
  == MEM ==
                total        used        free
  Mem:           62Gi        47Gi       8.2Gi
  == GPU ==
  0, NVIDIA A100, 87%, 32.1GB, 40.0GB
  1, NVIDIA A100, 12%, 4.0GB, 40.0GB

  init_project.sh — 项目脚手架

  # 新建 project：建 dir + conda env + git init + README + .gitignore + 
  scripts/setup_env.sh
  ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/init_project.sh thermodse_v2

  # Python 3.10 env 而非默认 3.11
  ... thermodse_v2 --py=3.10

  # 看现有项目 + conda envs
  ... --list

  # 跳过 git 或跳过 conda
  ... thermodse_v2 --no-git
  ... thermodse_v2 --no-conda

  sync.sh — Local ↔ Cluster 同步（您强调的新规则）

  # 1) 创建本地 mirror 子目录（一次性）
  ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/sync.sh --init-mirror
  # 在 ~/mirror/ 下生成 ~/mirror/<project>/ 子目录

  # 2) 推本地修改 → cluster (默认 push)
  ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/sync.sh ~/mirror/thermodse_v2
  thermodse_v2

  # 3) 拉远程 → 本地（处理并发修改）
  ... --pull

  # 4) 双向 sync (last-write-wins)
  ... --bidir

  # 5) **watch mode** — 任何 local 改动自动 push（您强调 "持续" 同步）
  ... --watch
  # 需要 brew install fswatch

  Watcher 每秒 fs-event 触发一次 push。比 git push 频繁得多 — 但只对本地 Mac 
  改源码有效；cluster 端的 GPU 训练输出（不在 git 里）不会被这条路径动。

  SKILL.md + README.md — 给 Claude / 给 user 的说明文档

  ---
  4 条 user-mandated rule 全部编码到 skill 行为里

  ┌───────────────────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │             Rule              │                  实现                   │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ 1. 以后都在 /home/ynwang/jhn/ │ workspace.sh hard-codes                 │
  │  下跑                         │ REMOTE_DIR=/home/ynwang/jhn             │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                               │ init_project.sh runs conda create -n    │
  │ 2. conda env                  │ $projname python=3.11 -y; workspace.sh  │
  │ per-project（目前要新创建）   │ --activate 自动 conda activate          │
  │                               │ $projname                               │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ 3.                            │ sync.sh --watch (continues              │
  │ 本地代码和服务器代码同步一套  │ local→remote) 或 sync.sh --bidir (双向) │
  ├───────────────────────────────┼─────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ 4. 随时注意 GPU 和 CPU        │ workspace.sh --status (passive) + 自动  │
  │                               │ banner (before-command)                 │
  └───────────────────────────────┴─────────────────────────────────────────┘

  ---
  三 skill 之间的关系

  ┌─────────────── research23-workspace ───────────────┐
  │  (workspace, init_project, sync — runtime rules)   │
  └────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────┘
                       │ depends on
                       ▼
             ┌──────── ssh-research23 ──────────┐
             │  (connect, sshpass, keepalive,    │
             │   2-hop proxy through research22) │
             └────────────────────────────────────┘

  research23-workspace 完全 wrap ssh-research23，后者只是底层 transport。

  ---
  立即可验证（4 步）

  # 1. SSH 还活着 + 密码没变
  RESEARCH23_PWD='!Wyn020214' ~/.claude/skills/ssh-research23/connect.sh
  --dry-run

  # 2. Init mirror
  RESEARCH23_PWD='!Wyn020214' ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/sync.sh
  --init-mirror

  # 3. 看 GPU + CPU
  RESEARCH23_PWD='!Wyn020214' ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/workspace.sh
  --status

  # 4. 进项目并 echo
  RESEARCH23_PWD='!Wyn020214' ~/.claude/skills/research23-workspace/workspace.sh
  --activate <proj> bash

  或者一次性 store 密码进 shell rcfile:

  echo 'export RESEARCH23_PWD="!Wyn020214"' >> ~/.zshrc
  source ~/.zshrc

  （不要装进 ~/.ssh/config 或 commit-able 的任何文件 — 那个 ! 在 bash history
  容易出 bug）

      24 +## Channel selection (2026-07-18 update)                       
      25 +                                                               
      26 +User is often NOT at HKU campus, and research22 proxy may be do

      27 +                                                               
      28 +| Channel | When | Mechanism |                                 
      29 +|---|---|---|                                                  
      30 +| `direct` (default) | off-campus / proxy down / fastest | sshp
         +ass -e ssh -o ProxyCommand=none → ynwang@research23.saas.hku.hk
         +:22 |                                                          
      31 +| `proxy` | on-campus / proxy alive / proxy preferred | uses ~/
         +.ssh/config `research23` Host alias with ProxyCommand |        
      32 +| `auto` (inferred) | best-effort | try direct first, fall back
         + to proxy if direct times out |                                
      33 +                                                               
      34 +Set via:                                                       
      35 +- env var: `RESEARCH23_TRANSPORT=direct|proxy|auto` (default: `
         +auto`)                                                         
      36 +- CLI flag: `connect.sh --direct | --proxy | --auto`           
      37 +- Default when both unset: `auto`                              
      38 +                                                               
      39 +The `direct` channel bypasses `~/.ssh/config`'s `research23` Ho
         +st alias entirely. This is important because if research22 prox
         +y is unreachable, the proxy channel fails with `Connection clos
         +ed by UNKNOWN port 65535`.                                     
      40 +                                                               
      41  ## Security model
      42  
      43  - **Passwords are NEVER hardcoded in this skill.** They're eith
          er:

  Thought for 10s (ctrl+o to expand)
